    "# Objectif\n", 
    "L'objectif de cette note est de montrer le nouveau design de SimFin. SimFin\n", 
    "est composé d'un module `simulator` qui est similaire à celui qu'on avait\n", 
    "auparavant. Mais il est accompagné d'un module qui permet de faire des\n", 
    "réplications en calcul parallel, `replicator`. Le module de `macro` a aussi\n", 
    "été complètement revue afin de simplifier la modélisation et prendre en\n", 
    "compte les cycles économiques." 
   ],

    "import numpy as np\n", 
    "from matplotlib import pyplot as plt\n", 
    "import pandas as pd"

   "cell_type": "markdown", 
   "source": [ 
    "Le code du module simulator est donné par :\n", 
    "\n", 
    "```\n", 
    "\n", 
    "import pandas as pd\n", 
    "import numpy as np\n", 
    "from matplotlib import pyplot as plt\n", 
    "import os\n", 
    "module_dir = os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(__file__))\n", 
    "import functools\n", 
    "import time\n", 
    "from simfin import profiler, macro\n", 
    "\n", 
    "class simulator:\n", 
    "    \"\"\"\n", 
    "    Classe principale pour contrôler le simulateur.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "    Cette classe permet d'initialiser les paramètres et réaliser des simulations.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "    Parameters\n", 
    "    ----------\n", 
    "    start_yr: int\n", 
    "        année de départ de la projection\n", 
    "    stop_yr: int\n", 
    "        année de fin de la projection\n", 
    "    \"\"\"\n", 
    "    def __init__(self,start_yr,stop_yr,stochastic=True):\n", 
    "        if start_yr>2021 :\n", 
    "            raise ValueError('La simulation doit commencer en 2021 ou avant...')\n", 
    "        else:\n", 
    "            self.start_yr = 2021\n", 
    "        self.stop_yr = stop_yr\n", 
    "        self.year = self.start_yr\n", 
    "        self.maxyrs = self.stop_yr - self.start_yr + 1\n", 
    "        self.set_pop()\n", 
    "        self.set_profiles()\n", 
    "        self.set_macro(stochastic)\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "    def set_pop(self,pop=None,file_pop='/simfin/params/simpop.csv'):\n", 
    "        if pop!=None:\n", 
    "            self.pop = pop\n", 
    "        else :\n", 
    "            self.pop = pd.read_csv(module_dir+file_pop,sep=';')\n", 
    "        self.pop = self.pop.set_index(['age', 'educ','insch','male','nkids','married'])\n", 
    "        self.pop = self.pop[[str(x) for x in range(self.start_yr,self.stop_yr+1)]]\n", 
    "        self.pop.columns = [int(x) for x in self.pop.columns]\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "    def set_profiles(self):\n", 
    "        self.profiles = profiler(self.pop.index)\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "    def set_macro(self,stochastic):\n", 
    "        self.macro = macro(self.start_yr,self.stop_yr,stochastic)\n", 
    "        self.macro.set_align(self.pop[self.start_yr],self.profiles.eco)\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "    def next(self):\n", 
    "        self.profiles.update()\n", 
    "        if self.year >= self.start_yr:\n", 
    "            self.macro.grow(self.year,self.pop[self.year],self.profiles.eco)\n", 
    "        self.year +=1\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "    def simulate(self):\n", 
    "        while (self.year < self.stop_yr):\n", 
    "            self.next()\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "    def reset(self):\n", 
    "        self.year = self.start_yr\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "```\n", 
    "On peut voir que la fonction d'initialisation prend les inputs habituels mais\n", 
    " aussi un flag pour déterminer si la simulation est stochastique.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "La fonction d'initialisation charge la population, les profils économiques et\n", 
    " le module macro que nous verrons plus tard.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "La population peut être soit celle par défault, ou une population qu'on entre\n", 
    " nous même. Ceci facilite d'introduire de nouveaux scénarios.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "Les profiles sont chargés par un module qui s'appelle `profiler`.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "La fonction `next()` permet de sauter d'une année à l'autre. Pour le moment,\n", 
    "il n'y a que les aggrégats économiques qui sont modifiés par ceci.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "La fonction `simulate()` est celle qui execute la simulation de l'année de\n", 
    "départ à l'année de fin. Finalement, la fonction `reset()` permet de\n", 
    "ré-initialiser." 
   ],

   "cell_type": "markdown", 
   "source": [ 
    "La module `replicator()` permet de faire plusieurs réplications de\n", 
    "simulations, avec par exemple des chocs différents à chaque réplication.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "La classe est donnée par\n", 
    "\n", 
    "```\n", 
    "from simfin import simulator\n", 
    "from copy import deepcopy\n", 
    "from multiprocessing import Pool as pool\n", 
    "from multiprocessing import cpu_count\n", 
    "import psutil\n", 
    "import ray\n", 
    "\n", 
    "@ray.remote\n", 
    "def run_model(m):\n", 
    "\tm.simulate()\n", 
    "\treturn m\n", 
    "\n", 
    "class replicator:\n", 
    "\tdef __init__(self,nreps,ncpus):\n", 
    "\t\tself.nreps = nreps\n", 
    "\t\tself.ncpus = ncpus\n", 
    "\tdef set_model(self,model):\n", 
    "\t\tself.models = []\n", 
    "\t\tfor m in range(self.nreps):\n", 
    "\t\t\tself.models.append(deepcopy(model))\n", 
    "\n", 
    "\tdef replicate(self):\n", 
    "\t\tif self.ncpus>1:\n", 
    "\t\t\tray.shutdown()\n", 
    "\t\t\tray.init(num_cpus=self.ncpus,ignore_reinit_error=True)\n", 
    "\t\t\tself.models = ray.get([run_model.remote(m) for m in self.models])\n", 
    "\t\telse :\n", 
    "\t\t\tself.models = [run_model.remote(m) for m in self.models]\n", 
    "\t\treturn\n", 
    "\n", 
    "```\n", 
    "\n", 
    "Cette classe utilise le module python `ray` qui permet de faire du calcul\n", 
    "parallel. On définit d'abord le nombre de réplication et le nombre de CPU\n", 
    "disponible pour le calcul dans la fonction d'initialision. La deuxième\n", 
    "fonction permet de définir le modèle qui est une instance de `simulator`. La\n", 
    "classe `replicator` en fait des copies. Ceci permet beaucoup de flexibilité\n", 
    "mais prendra beaucoup de mémoire si un grand nombre de réplications est\n", 
    "choisi. C'est un arbitrage qu'on pourra revoir. Finalement la fonction\n", 
    "`replicate()` est celle qui exécute chaque instance et récolte les résultats.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "On exécute ici-bas 20 réplications avec 8 CPU (il faudra adapter à votre\n", 
    "environnement). Il est à noter que ceci devrait fonctionner sur Harold et\n", 
    "Maude sans trop de difficulté.\n", 
    "\n" 
   ],

    "On voudra regarder les autres modules. Le module profiler est très similaire\n", 
    "pour le moment au code qu'on avait avant. Par contre, le module `macro` a\n", 
    "bien évolué.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "Voici la fonction d'initialisation,\n", 
    "\n", 
    "```\n", 
    "class macro:\n", 
    "    def __init__(self,start_yr, stop_yr,stochastic=True):\n", 
    "        self.start_yr = start_yr\n", 
    "        self.stop_yr = stop_yr\n", 
    "        self.stochastic = stochastic\n", 
    "        self.load_aggregates()\n", 
    "        self.set_shocks()\n", 
    "        self.set_gr_YperH_rates()\n", 
    "        self.set_infl_rate()\n", 
    "        self.set_sp500()\n", 
    "        self.set_b1yr_rates()\n", 
    "        self.set_b5yr_spread()\n", 
    "        self.set_b10yr_spread()\n", 
    "        self.set_b30yr_spread()\n", 
    "        self.set_infl_rate()\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "```\n", 
    "\n", 
    "La fonction va charger les données historiques trimestrielles et annuelles,\n", 
    "estimer le modèle VAR pour les chocs et poser les hypothèses de croissances\n", 
    "de long-terme des aggrégats macro."

    "Maintenant regardons la fonction qui charge l'historique macro.\n",

    "```\n", 
    "    def load_aggregates(self):\n", 
    "        self.hist_aggr_q = pd.read_excel(\n", 
    "            module_dir+'/simfin/params/macro_q.xlsx',sheet_name='data')\n",

    "                                          'gr_H','gr_Yp','gr_YperH'])\n", 
    "        return\n",

    "\n", 
    "La fonction charge d'abord les données macro annuelles sur les aggrégats. Ces\n", 
    " aggrégats sont surtout utiles pour initialiser le modèle. Les aggrégats sont\n",

    "  l'année de départ sera simulé. Le PIB potentiel est supposé égal au PIB\n", 
    "  nominal. On fait cette hypothèse puisqu'on veut surtout la croissance du\n", 
    "  PIB potentiel pour faire croitre certains postes fiscaux sans les faire\n", 
    "  varier avec le cycle économique. La variable du niveau du potentiel n'est\n", 
    "  pas vraiment nécessaire.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "Les données trimestrielles permettront d'estimer la structure des chocs.\n",

    "On y reviendra."

   "source": [ 
    "La fonction d'initialisation des chocs est de loin la plus compliquée. On y\n", 
    "estimera un VAR(1) des variables macro trimestrielles. On utilise la\n", 
    "croissance du PIB par heure travaillé, des heures travaillées, l'inflation,\n", 
    "le taux de rendement boursier, le taux obligataire du Québec à 1 an ainsi que\n", 
    " les écarts pour les taux à 5ans (par rapport à 1), 10 ans (par rapport à 5\n", 
    " ans) et finalement 30 ans (par rapport à 10 ans).\n", 
    "\n", 
    "On débute par créer des dummy saisonnières. Ensuite on crée les écarts de\n", 
    "taux. Finalement, on crée la croissance de la productivité et des heures\n", 
    "travaillées.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "Pour chacune de ces séries, on utilise le filtre Hodrick-Prescott pour\n", 
    "séparer la tendance du cycle. On va modéliser le cycle à l'aide d'un VAR. On\n", 
    "va plutôt utiliser des hypothèses de long-terme directement dans les\n", 
    "projections. On estime le VAR avec des effets trimestrielles et on sauvegarde\n", 
    " les paramètres.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "Finalement, on initialise le choc de départ en utilisant Q4 de 2020 comme\n", 
    "valeur d'intialisation des chocs. Il est à noter que pour plusieurs des\n", 
    "aggrégats, la valeur de départ de la croissance de long-terme sera basé sur\n", 
    "la tendance estimée par le filtre HP.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "\n", 
    "\n", 
    "```\n", 
    "    def set_shocks(self):\n", 
    "        df = self.hist_aggr_q.loc[:,:]\n", 
    "        df = df.reset_index()\n", 
    "        for q in range(1, 5):\n", 
    "            df['quarter_' + str(q)] = np.where(df['q'] == q, 1, 0)\n", 
    "        df['spread5yr'] = df['b5yr'] - df['b1yr']\n", 
    "        df['spread10yr'] = df['b10yr'] - df['b5yr']\n", 
    "        df['spread30yr'] = df['b30yr'] - df['b10yr']\n", 
    "        df['gr_YperH'] = df['YperH']/df['YperH'].shift(1)-1\n", 
    "        df['gr_H'] = df['H']/df['H'].shift(1)-1\n", 
    "        outcomes = ['gr_YperH','gr_H','infl','sp500','b1yr','spread5yr','spread10yr',\n", 
    "                  'spread30yr']\n", 
    "        for o in outcomes:\n", 
    "            c, t = hp(df[o].dropna())\n", 
    "            df.loc[~df[o].isna(),o + '_t'] = t\n", 
    "            df.loc[~df[o].isna(),o + '_c'] = c\n", 
    "        outcomes_c = [c+'_c' for c in  outcomes]\n", 
    "        outcomes_t = [c + '_t' for c in outcomes]\n", 
    "        dates = df[['year', 'q']].astype(int).astype(str)\n", 
    "        quarterly = dates[\"year\"] + \"Q\" + dates[\"q\"]\n", 
    "        quarterly = dates_from_str(quarterly)\n", 
    "        df.index = pd.DatetimeIndex(quarterly)\n", 
    "        self.df_for_shocks = df\n", 
    "        data = df.dropna()\n", 
    "        data_est = data.loc[(data.index.year<=2019),:]\n", 
    "        model = VAR(data_est[outcomes_c],exog=data_est[['quarter_2',\n", 
    "                                                        'quarter_3',\n", 
    "                                            'quarter_4']])\n", 
    "        results = model.fit(1)\n", 
    "        lags = results.coefs\n", 
    "        params = pd.DataFrame(index=outcomes, columns=outcomes,\n", 
    "                              data=lags[0, :, :])\n", 
    "        const = results.coefs_exog\n", 
    "        exog_params = pd.DataFrame(index=outcomes_c,\n", 
    "                                   columns=['const', 'q2', 'q3', 'q4'],\n", 
    "                                   data=const)\n", 
    "        for q in [2,3,4]:\n", 
    "            exog_params['const_q'+str(q)] = exog_params['const'] + \\\n", 
    "                                           exog_params['q'+str(q)]\n", 
    "        exog_params['const_q1'] = exog_params['const']\n", 
    "        const = ['const_q' + str(q) for q in range(1, 5)]\n", 
    "        icepts = exog_params[const]\n", 
    "        icepts.index = outcomes\n", 
    "        icepts.columns = [1,2,3,4]\n", 
    "        covar = results.resid.cov()\n", 
    "        covar = pd.DataFrame(index=outcomes_c, columns=outcomes_c, data=covar)\n", 
    "        covar.index = outcomes\n", 
    "        covar.columns = outcomes\n", 
    "        self.shocks = shocks(icepts,params,covar,self.stochastic)\n", 
    "        # initializing\n", 
    "        period = (data.index.year==2020) & (data.index.quarter==4)\n", 
    "        last_shocks = data.loc[period,outcomes_c].iloc[0,:]\n", 
    "        last_shocks.index = outcomes\n", 
    "        self.shocks.start_from(last_shocks)\n", 
    "        last_trend = data.loc[period,outcomes_t].iloc[0,:]\n", 
    "        last_trend.index = outcomes\n", 
    "        self.last_trend = last_trend\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    " ```" 
   ],

  { 
   "cell_type": "markdown", 
   "source": [ 
    "La classe `shock` ne fait qu'appliquer le VAR. Elle est très générale et\n", 
    "permet de simuler simplement à partir du VAR.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "```\n", 
    "class shocks:\n", 
    "    def __init__(self,alpha,Phi,V,stochastic):\n", 
    "        self.alpha = alpha.to_numpy()\n", 
    "        self.Phi = Phi.to_numpy()\n", 
    "        self.V = V.to_numpy()\n", 
    "        self.outcomes = Phi.columns.to_list()\n", 
    "        self.J = len(self.outcomes)\n", 
    "        if stochastic:\n", 
    "            self.L = np.linalg.cholesky(self.V)\n", 
    "        else :\n", 
    "            self.L = np.zeros((self.J,self.J))\n", 
    "        self.nq = 4\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "    def start_from(self,last_shocks):\n", 
    "        self.state = last_shocks\n", 
    "    def update_one_q(self,q):\n", 
    "        state = self.state.to_numpy().reshape((self.J,1))\n", 
    "\n", 
    "        eps = np.random.normal(size=self.J).reshape((self.J,1))\n", 
    "        next_state = self.alpha[:,q-1].reshape((self.J,1)) + self.Phi @ state\\\n", 
    "                     + self.L @ eps\n", 
    "        self.state = pd.Series(index = self.state.index, data = next_state[:,0])\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "    def update_1yr(self):\n", 
    "        register = pd.DataFrame(index=self.state.index,columns = [x for x in\n", 
    "                                                                  range(1,5)])\n", 
    "        for q in range(1,5):\n", 
    "            self.update_one_q(q)\n", 
    "            register.loc[:,q] = self.state.to_list()\n", 
    "        return register\n", 
    "\n", 
    "```\n" 
   ], 
   "metadata": { 
    "collapsed": false, 
    "pycharm": { 
     "name": "#%% md\n" 
    }

    "Une série de fonction fixe les hypothèses de long-terme sur les différents\n", 
    "aggrégats. Ceci est composé d'une valeur de départ, une valeur à long-terme et l'année à laquelle cette valeur de\n", 
    "long-terme est réalisée.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "    def set_gr_YperH_rates(self,current_rate=0.035,lt_rate=0.015, catch_yr =\n", 
    "        2025):\n", 
    "        self.base_gr_YperH = pd.Series(index=np.arange(self.start_yr,\n", 
    "                                                     self.stop_yr))\n", 
    "        self.base_gr_YperH[self.start_yr] = current_rate\n", 
    "        slope = (lt_rate - current_rate)/(catch_yr - self.start_yr)\n", 
    "        for yr in range(self.start_yr+1,self.stop_yr):\n", 
    "                if yr<=catch_yr:\n", 
    "                    self.base_gr_YperH[yr] = current_rate + slope*(yr -\n", 
    "                                                              self.start_yr)\n", 
    "                else :\n", 
    "                    self.base_gr_YperH[yr] = lt_rate\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "    def set_b1yr_rates(self,lt_rate=0.01, catch_yr = 2035):\n", 
    "        current_rate = self.last_trend['b1yr']\n", 
    "        self.base_b1yr = pd.Series(index=np.arange(self.start_yr,self.stop_yr))\n", 
    "        self.base_b1yr[self.start_yr] = current_rate\n", 
    "        slope = (lt_rate - current_rate)/(catch_yr - self.start_yr)\n", 
    "        for yr in range(self.start_yr+1,self.stop_yr):\n", 
    "                if yr<=catch_yr:\n", 
    "                    self.base_b1yr[yr] = current_rate + slope*(yr - self.start_yr)\n", 
    "                else :\n", 
    "                    self.base_b1yr[yr] = lt_rate\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "    def set_b5yr_spread(self,lt_rate = 0.01,catch_yr=2035):\n", 
    "        current_rate = self.last_trend['spread5yr']\n", 
    "        self.base_b5yr_spread = pd.Series(index=np.arange(self.start_yr,\n", 
    "                                                     self.stop_yr))\n", 
    "        self.base_b5yr_spread[self.start_yr] = current_rate\n", 
    "        slope = (lt_rate - current_rate)/(catch_yr - self.start_yr)\n", 
    "        for yr in range(self.start_yr+1,self.stop_yr):\n", 
    "                if yr<=catch_yr:\n", 
    "                    self.base_b5yr_spread[yr] = current_rate + slope*(yr -\n", 
    "                                                               self.start_yr)\n", 
    "                else :\n", 
    "                    self.base_b5yr_spread[yr] = lt_rate\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "    def set_b10yr_spread(self,lt_rate = 0.01,catch_yr=2035):\n", 
    "        current_rate = self.last_trend['spread10yr']\n", 
    "        self.base_b10yr_spread = pd.Series(index=np.arange(self.start_yr,\n", 
    "                                                     self.stop_yr))\n", 
    "        self.base_b10yr_spread[self.start_yr] = current_rate\n", 
    "        slope = (lt_rate - current_rate)/(catch_yr - self.start_yr)\n", 
    "        for yr in range(self.start_yr+1,self.stop_yr):\n", 
    "                if yr<=catch_yr:\n", 
    "                    self.base_b10yr_spread[yr] = current_rate + slope*(yr -\n", 
    "                                                               self.start_yr)\n", 
    "                else :\n", 
    "                    self.base_b10yr_spread[yr] = lt_rate\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "    def set_b30yr_spread(self,lt_rate = 0.01,catch_yr=2035):\n", 
    "        current_rate = self.last_trend['spread30yr']\n", 
    "        self.base_b30yr_spread = pd.Series(index=np.arange(self.start_yr,\n", 
    "                                                     self.stop_yr))\n", 
    "        self.base_b30yr_spread[self.start_yr] = current_rate\n", 
    "        slope = (lt_rate - current_rate)/(catch_yr - self.start_yr)\n", 
    "        for yr in range(self.start_yr+1,self.stop_yr):\n", 
    "                if yr<=catch_yr:\n", 
    "                    self.base_b30yr_spread[yr] = current_rate + slope*(yr -\n", 
    "                                                               self.start_yr)\n", 
    "                else :\n", 
    "                    self.base_b30yr_spread[yr] = lt_rate\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "    def set_sp500(self,lt_rate=0.07,catch_yr = 2025):\n", 
    "        current_rate = (1.0+self.last_trend['sp500'])**4-1\n", 
    "        self.base_sp500 = pd.Series(index=np.arange(self.start_yr,self.stop_yr))\n", 
    "        self.base_sp500[self.start_yr] = current_rate\n", 
    "        slope = (lt_rate - current_rate)/(catch_yr - self.start_yr)\n", 
    "        for yr in range(self.start_yr+1,self.stop_yr):\n", 
    "                if yr<=catch_yr:\n", 
    "                    self.base_sp500[yr] = current_rate + slope*(yr - self.start_yr)\n", 
    "                else :\n", 
    "                    self.base_sp500[yr] = lt_rate\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "    def set_infl_rate(self,lt_rate=0.02,catch_yr = 2025):\n", 
    "        current_rate = (1.0+self.last_trend['infl'])**4-1\n", 
    "        self.base_inflrate = pd.Series(index=np.arange(self.start_yr,self.stop_yr))\n", 
    "        self.base_inflrate[self.start_yr] = current_rate\n", 
    "        slope = (lt_rate - current_rate)/(catch_yr - self.start_yr)\n", 
    "        for yr in range(self.start_yr+1,self.stop_yr):\n", 
    "                if yr<=catch_yr:\n", 
    "                    self.base_inflrate[yr] = current_rate + slope*(yr - self.start_yr)\n", 
    "                else :\n", 
    "                    self.base_inflrate[yr] = lt_rate\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "```"

   "cell_type": "markdown", 
   "source": [ 
    "La prochaine fonction permet durant la simulation de créer les taux de\n", 
    "croissance annuel à partir des tendances de long-terme, de la structure de la\n", 
    "population et finalement des chocs.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "La croissance de tendance est d'abord ramené sur une base trimestrielle. Par\n", 
    "la suite, on applique les chocs. Tout dépendant de la variable, ceci sera\n", 
    "implémenté en taux composé ou non. Pour les taux obligataires, on prend une\n", 
    "moyenne des chocs pour le taux annuel. Chaque taux annuel est ensuite\n", 
    "sauvegardé dans une variable globale.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "```\n", 
    "    def update_rates(self,yr,eco,pop):\n", 
    "        # base rates for that year\n", 
    "        shocks = self.shocks.update_1yr()\n", 
    "        # productivity growth rate\n", 
    "        gr_YperH_t = (1+self.base_gr_YperH[yr])**(1/4)-1\n", 
    "        if self.stochastic:\n", 
    "            gr_YperH_c = shocks.loc['gr_YperH',:].to_numpy()\n", 
    "        else :\n", 
    "            gr_YperH_c = np.zeros(4)\n", 
    "        gr_YperH = 1.0\n", 
    "        for q in range(4):\n", 
    "            gr_YperH *= (1.0+gr_YperH_t + gr_YperH_c[q])\n", 
    "        self.gr_YperH = gr_YperH-1\n", 
    "        # hours growth rate\n", 
    "        H = self.align*pop.multiply(eco['emp']*eco['hours_c'],\n", 
    "                                  fill_value=0.0).sum()\n", 
    "        gr_H_t = H / self.H - 1\n", 
    "        self.gr_H_p = gr_H_t\n", 
    "        # compute growth rate if hours\n", 
    "        gr_H_t = (1+gr_H_t)**(1/4)-1\n", 
    "        if self.stochastic:\n", 
    "            gr_H_c = shocks.loc['gr_H',:].to_numpy()\n", 
    "        else :\n", 
    "            gr_H_c = np.zeros(4)\n", 
    "        gr_H = 1.0\n", 
    "        for q in range(4):\n", 
    "            gr_H *= (1.0+gr_H_t + gr_H_c[q])\n", 
    "        self.gr_H = gr_H-1\n", 
    "        # inflation\n", 
    "        infl_t = (1+self.base_inflrate[yr])**(1/4)-1\n", 
    "        if self.stochastic:\n", 
    "            infl_c = shocks.loc['infl',:].to_numpy()\n", 
    "        else :\n", 
    "            infl_c = np.zeros(4)\n", 
    "        infl = 1.0\n", 
    "        for q in range(4):\n", 
    "            infl *= (1.0+infl_t + infl_c[q])\n", 
    "        self.inflrate = infl-1\n", 
    "        # sp 500 returns\n", 
    "        sp500_t = (1+self.base_sp500[yr])**(1/4)-1\n", 
    "        if self.stochastic:\n", 
    "            sp500_c = shocks.loc['sp500',:].to_numpy()\n", 
    "        else :\n", 
    "            sp500_c = np.zeros(4)\n", 
    "        sp500 = 1.0\n", 
    "        for q in range(4):\n", 
    "            sp500 *= (1.0+sp500_t + sp500_c[q])\n", 
    "        self.sp500 = sp500-1\n", 
    "        # b1yr returns\n", 
    "        b1yr_t = self.base_b1yr[yr]\n", 
    "        if self.stochastic:\n", 
    "            b1yr_c = shocks.loc['b1yr',:].to_numpy()\n", 
    "        else :\n", 
    "            b1yr_c = np.zeros(4)\n", 
    "        b1yr = b1yr_t + np.mean(b1yr_c)\n", 
    "        self.b1yr = b1yr\n", 
    "        # b5yr returns\n", 
    "        b5yr_t = b1yr + self.base_b5yr_spread[yr]\n", 
    "        if self.stochastic:\n", 
    "            b5yr_c = shocks.loc['spread5yr',:].to_numpy()\n", 
    "        else :\n", 
    "            b5yr_c = np.zeros(4)\n", 
    "        b5yr = b5yr_t + np.mean(b5yr_c)\n", 
    "        self.b5yr = b5yr\n", 
    "        # b10yr returns\n", 
    "        b10yr_t = b5yr + self.base_b10yr_spread[yr]\n", 
    "        if self.stochastic:\n", 
    "            b10yr_c = shocks.loc['spread10yr',:].to_numpy()\n", 
    "        else :\n", 
    "            b10yr_c = np.zeros(4)\n", 
    "        b10yr = b10yr_t + np.mean(b10yr_c)\n", 
    "        self.b10yr = b10yr\n", 
    "        # b30yr returns\n", 
    "        b30yr_t = b10yr + self.base_b30yr_spread[yr]\n", 
    "        if self.stochastic:\n", 
    "            b30yr_c = shocks.loc['spread30yr',:].to_numpy()\n", 
    "        else :\n", 
    "            b30yr_c = np.zeros(4)\n", 
    "        b30yr = b30yr_t + np.mean(b30yr_c)\n", 
    "        self.b30yr = b30yr\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "\n", 
    "```\n"

   "source": [ 
    "La fonction d'alignement permet de s'assurer que les heures travaillées\n", 
    "prédite en appliquant la structure de la population et les profils donne les\n", 
    "heures travaillées aggrégées.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "```\n", 
    "    def set_align(self,pop,eco):\n", 
    "        H = pop.multiply(eco['emp']*eco['hours_c'],fill_value=0.0).sum()\n", 
    "        self.align = self.H/H\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "```" 
   ], 
   "metadata": { 
    "collapsed": false, 
    "pycharm": { 
     "name": "#%% md\n" 
    } 
   } 
  }, 
  { 
   "cell_type": "markdown", 
   "source": [ 
    "La fonction de croissance permet ensuite de faire crôitre les aggrégats.\n", 
    "\n", 
    "```\n", 
    "    def grow(self,yr,pop,eco):\n", 
    "        # generate shocks\n", 
    "        self.update_rates(yr,eco,pop)\n", 
    "        # compute population\n", 
    "        self.N = pop.sum()\n", 
    "        # compute total hours worked\n", 
    "        self.H *= (1+self.gr_H)\n", 
    "        # Employment\n", 
    "        self.E = pop.multiply(eco['emp'],fill_value=0.0).sum()\n", 
    "        # create new potentiel and actual GDP\n", 
    "        self.Yp *= (1.0 + self.gr_H_p + self.base_gr_YperH[yr] + self.inflrate)\n", 
    "        self.Y *= (1.0 + self.gr_H + self.gr_YperH + self.inflrate)\n", 
    "        gr_Y = self.gr_H + self.gr_YperH + self.inflrate\n", 
    "        self.gr_Y = gr_Y\n", 
    "        self.gr_Yp = self.gr_H_p + self.base_gr_YperH[yr] + self.inflrate\n", 
    "        # wage growth\n", 
    "        self.gr_wage = self.gr_Y - self.gr_H\n", 
    "        # keep in table\n", 
    "        self.to_aggr(yr)\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    " ```" 
   ], 
   "metadata": { 
    "collapsed": false, 
    "pycharm": { 
     "name": "#%% md\n" 
    } 
   },

     "ename": "SyntaxError", 
     "evalue": "invalid syntax (<ipython-input-8-98b017f5a6fc>, line 1)",

   "cell_type": "markdown", 
   "source": [ 
    "Et finalement sauvegarder les aggrégats et autres quantités.\n", 
    "\n", 
    " ```\n", 
    "    def to_aggr(self,yr):\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'Y'] = self.Y\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'Yp'] = self.Yp\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'N'] = self.N\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'H'] = self.H\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'E'] = self.E\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'gr_wage'] = self.gr_wage\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'infl'] = self.inflrate\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'YperH'] = self.Y/self.H\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'sp500'] = self.sp500\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'b1yr'] = self.b1yr\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'b5yr'] = self.b5yr\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'b10yr'] = self.b10yr\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'b30yr'] = self.b30yr\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'gr_Y'] = self.gr_Y\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'gr_Yp'] = self.gr_Yp\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'gr_H'] = self.gr_H\n", 
    "        self.aggr.loc[yr,'gr_YperH'] = self.gr_YperH\n", 
    "        return\n", 
    "```\n"
